TITLE       Neutron-capture cross-sections of 244Cm and 246Cm     2314100100003 
           measured with an array of large germanium detectors in 2314100100004 
           the ANNRI at J-PARC/MLF.                               2314100100005

REL-REF    (I,,K.Kino+,J,NIM/A,626,58,2011)                       2314100100029 
           Measurement of energy spectra and spatial distributions2314100100030 
           of neutron beams provided by the ANNRI beamline for    2314100100031 
           capture cross-section measurements at the J-PARC/MLF,  2314100100032 
FACILITY   (SYNCH,2JPNJAE) The neutron-nucleus reaction instrument2314100100033 
            (NNRI) at the J-PARC MLF Beam Line No. 4 (BL04).      2314100100034 
            Accelerator was operated in double-bunch mode at a    2314100100035 
           beam power of 120 kW and a repetition rate of 25 Hz.   2314100100036 
           Disk chopper with a semicircular shape was used to     2314100100037 
           prevent the intrusion of the low-energy tail of neutron2314100100038 
           pulse into the next pulse duration.                    2314100100039 
METHOD     (TOF) Flight length 21.502+-0.005 m.                   2314100100040 
           Disk chopper with semicircular shape was installed at  2314100100041 
           flight length of 14 m to exclude the effect from       2314100100042 
           overlapping neutrons.                                  2314100100043 
           Data were measured with event-by-event mode storing the2314100100044 
           information of gamma-ray pulse height (PHA), TOF and   2314100100045 
           time-interval between coincidence signals.             2314100100046 
            Time resolution of DAQ system is 10 ns.               2314100100047 
INC-SOURCE (SPALL) Pulsed neutron beam was collimated to diameter 2314100100048 
           of 7 mm at the sample position. Proton energy 3 GeV,   2314100100049 
           average beam power 120 kW, repetition rate 25 Hz.      2314100100050 
           Proton intensity of shots was stable within 1% in FWHM.2314100100051 
           Primary neutron production target - mercury.           2314100100052 
           Time resolution of proton beam 600ns (The proton beams 2314100100053 
           were supplied in the "double-bunch mode," each bunch   2314100100054 
           with a width of 100 ns, at intervals of 600 ns).       2314100100055 
           Para H as moderator of 1400 mm diameter, 120 mm height.2314100100056 
DETECTOR   (D4PI,GE,BGO) 4PI Ge spectrometer: two cluster-Ge      2314100100057 
           detectors and eight coaxial Ge detectors surrounded by 2314100100058 
           BGO anti-Compton shields. Set at a position 21.5m from 2314100100059 
           the neutron source. To detect the prompt gamma-rays.   2314100100060 
           In the present measurement only two cluster Ge         2314100100061 
           detectors (each of 7 Ge crystals) were used.           2314100100062 
           To suppress the gamma-flash effect to the detector,    2314100100063 
           Pb filter of 37.5 mm thickness was inserted into the   2314100100064 
           flight path.                                           2314100100065 
           The sample was set in Al beam duct. To decrease        2314100100066 
           background scattering from N-14 and O-16, the duct was 2314100100067 
           filled with He gas. Lithium hydride powder in Al       2314100100068 
           containers, sheets of boron and rubber mixture, lead   2314100100069 
           plates of 3 mm thickness were set between the beam duct2314100100070 
           and the cluster Ge detectors to protect scattered      2314100100071 
           neutrons and decay gamma-rays from the high-activity   2314100100072 
           Cm-244 sample. The detectors were covered with         2314100100073 
           radiation shield of lead, iron, and boron resin.       2314100100074 
           Gamma-ray signals from the 14 Ge crystals in the       2314100100075 
           cluster Ge detectors were acquired using an original   2314100100076 
           data acquisition (DAQ) system based on a digital data  2314100100077 
           processing technique.                                  2314100100078 
           Random pulse generator (Berkeley Nucleonics, DB-2) was 2314100100079 
           used to estimate the dead time of detectors.           2314100100080 
           The total efficiency of the 4PI Ge spectrometer for the2314100100081 
           entire energy region was less than 12%, as calculated  2314100100082 
           using standard gamma-ray sources (Cs-137, Co-60) and   2314100100083 
           the EGS5 Monte Carlo simulation code.                  2314100100084 
PART-DET   (G) Prompt gamma-rays.                                 2314100100085 
ANALYSIS   The neutron energy was calibrated by measuring a Au    2314100100086 
           sample with well-known neutron resonances.             2314100100087 
           Detection efficiency of capture gamma-rays for each    2314100100088 
           resonance was assumed to be constant.                  2314100100089 
            The relative yields were normalized at the first      2314100100090 
           resonance of 240Pu to the weighted evaluated values in 2314100100091 
           JENDL-4.0 by the abundance of 240Pu                    2314100100092 
CORRECTION For dead time - correction factor was obtained by using2314100100093 
           the random pulse generator. Dead time typically 5musec.2314100100094 
           For background due to overlapping neutron and decay    2314100100095 
           gamma rays and for neutron energy dependent background.2314100100096 
           For self-shielding and multiple-scattering effects by  2314100100097 
           the Monte Carlo simulation code MCNP.                  2314100100098 
           For influence of fission events.                       2314100100099 
MONITOR    (5-B-10(N,A)3-LI-7,PAR,SIG,G)                          2314100100100 
           Energy dependence of neutron flux was estimated from   2314100100101 
           the TOF spectrum gated at the 478 keV gamma-ray peak   2314100100102 
           emitted from the 10B(n,alpha gamma)7Li reaction.       2314100100103 
MONIT-REF  (,,3,JENDL-4.0,,2012)                                  2314100100104

REACTION   ((96-CM-244(N,G)96-CM-245,,SIG,,RES)//                 2314100200003 
           (96-CM-244(N,G)96-CM-245,,SIG,,RES))                   2314100200004 
SAMPLE     Cm-244 sample was composed of curium oxide powder      2314100200005 
           CmO2; weight 0.6 mg; activity 1.8 GBq and Al powder    2314100200006 
           (weight 25 mg) for dilution. The isotopic ratio of the 2314100200007 
           Cm sample measured by the Kyoto University Research    2314100200008 
           Reactor Institute (KURRI):                             2314100200009 
           Isotope    Spec. sheet          KURRI                  2314100200010 
           Cm-243     0.02                -                       2314100200011 
           Cm-244     82.42              89.57 +- 1.68            2314100200012 
           Cm-245     2.19                2.66 +- 0.34            2314100200013 
           Cm-246     5.86                7.08 +- 0.33            2314100200014 
           Cm-247     0.15                -                       2314100200015 
           Cm-248     0.11                -                       2314100200016 
           Sample was contained in Al case with an inner diameter 2314100200017 
           of 5mm and inner depth of 0.5 mm. The outer diameter of2314100200018 
           the Al case is 9mm and the thickness is 1.2 mm.        2314100200019 
           Cm sample was irradiated with neutron pulses of 2.6E+6 2314100200020 
           shots for 33 h.                                        2314100200021 
INC-SPECT   Background level of neutrons was negligible.          2314100200022 
           The obtained neutron flux is shown in Fig.2 of         2314100200023 
           J,NST,47,(12),1097,2010.                               2314100200024 
           Energy-integrated neutron intensities at sample        2314100200025 
           position are 4.5E+6 n/s/cm**2 in neutron energy range  2314100200026 
           1.5-25 meV, 6.6E+5 n/s/cm**2 in 0.9-1.1 keV.           2314100200027 
           The incident neutron flux shape was measured with      2314100200028 
           sintered natural boron sample (8.67 mg).               2314100200029 
DETECTOR   The peak efficiency of 4PI Ge spectrometer is          2314100200030 
            3.64+-0.11 % for 1.33-MeV gamma- rays.                2314100200031 
           Typical resolution is 9.8 keV (on beam) and 2.4 keV    2314100200032 
            (off beam) in FWHM for 1.33-MeV gamma-rays.           2314100200033 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-S) Statistical error.                             2314100200034 
           (ERR-1) Uncertainty due to the difference in the energy2314100200035 
           distribution of capture gamma-rays for each neutron    2314100200036 
           resonance, which contributes to the detection          2314100200037 
           efficiency.                                            2314100200038 
           (ERR-2) Uncertainty due to dead-time correction.       2314100200039 
           (ERR-3) Uncertainty due to multiplicity for the capture2314100200040 
             gamma-rays.                                          2314100200041 
           (ERR-SYS) Total systematical uncertainty.              2314100200042 
ADD-RES    (COMP) Comparison with JENDL-3.3 data.                 2314100200043 
           Ratios for En 85.96 and 96.12 eV are different from the2314100200044 
           evaluated values. In the former case, two resonances of2314100200045 
           85.96 (Cm-244C; foreground) and 84.62 eV (Cm-246;      2314100200046 
           background) overlap in the TOF spectrum; these two     2314100200047 
           resonance peaks are difficult to separate.In the latter2314100200048 
           case, 98.85 eV (248Cm; background) overlaps with the   2314100200049 
           foreground.                                            2314100200050

REACTION   (96-CM-244(N,G)96-CM-245,,SIG)                         2314100300003 
SAMPLE     Cm-244 sample was 0.6 mg of curium oxide.              2314100300004 
           Isotopic enrichment was 90.1 mole%, main activity was  2314100300005 
           1.8 GBq. Sample was sealed in an Al case of 9 mm outer 2314100300006 
           diameter, weighing 280 mg, 0.5-mm-thick walls.         2314100300007 
           Sample was put in a bag of fluorinated ethylene        2314100300008 
           propylene (FEP) films and attached to a sample holder  2314100300009 
           made of polytetrafluoroethylene and shaped into        2314100300010 
           50mmx70 mm rectangular frame.                          2314100300011 
           The isotopic abundances were determined by thermal     2314100300012 
           ionization mass spectrometry - TIMS (mole%) :          2314100300013 
           Cm-244 - 90.1  +- 1.7 , Cm-245 -  2.71 +- 0.34,        2314100300014 
           Cm-246 - 7.22  +- 0.34, Cm-247 -  not detected,        2314100300015 
           Cm-248 -  not detected.                                2314100300016 
           The isotopic abundances were determined by alpha-ray   2314100300017 
           spectrometry(normalized to results of 244Cm with TIMS):2314100300018 
           Cm-244 - 90.1, Cm-245 -  not detected,                 2314100300019 
           Cm-246 - 7.0  +- 0.6, Cm-247 -  not detected,          2314100300020 
           Cm-248 -  not detected, Pu-240 - 13.6 +- 0.6 .         2314100300021 
           Cm sample was irradiated 64 h.                         2314100300022 
           Am-243 abundance was obtained by fitting of normalized 2314100300023 
           yields at first resonance with code SAMMY-7 and was    2314100300024 
           defined to be (0.63+-0.04) % .                         2314100300025 
INC-SPECT  The energy integrated neutron intensities at the sample2314100300026 
           position are 5.2E+10 n/s/m2 in the neutron energy      2314100300027 
           range 1.5-25 meV and 7.2E+09 n/s/m2 in 0.9-1.1 keV     2314100300028 
           under a proton beam power of 120 kW.                   2314100300029 
ANALYSIS    The contributions from 244Cm were calculated by       2314100300030 
           subtracting the contributions from the impurities from 2314100300031 
           the capture yields.                                    2314100300032 
           Contributions from impurities of 240Pu, 243Am, 246Cm   2314100300033 
            (without 244Cm) were calculated with SAMMY using the  2314100300034 
           parameters of these work and JENDL-4.0.                2314100300035 
           Neutron-capture cross sections of 244Cm were obtained  2314100300036 
           by dividing the 244Cm contributions by the isotopic    2314100300037 
           ratio.                                                 2314100300038 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T,,,P) Total uncertainty.                         2314100300039 
           (ERR-S,,,U) Statistical Error.                         2314100300040 
           (ERR-1,,,F) Systematic Error in the normalization.     2314100300041 
           (ERR-2,,,U) Error in the contribution of capture events2314100300042 
                   of the other nuclei.                           2314100300043 
           (ERR-3,,,U) Error in the contribution of fission events2314100300044 
           (ERR-4,,,U) Error in the corrections of self-shielding 2314100300045 
                  and multiple scattering.                        2314100300046 
           (ERR-5,,,P) Other uncertainties (neutron flux,         2314100300047 
            contaminations of scattered events, deadtime          2314100300048 
            correction.                                           2314100300049 
            Non-neutron-energy-dependent errors are:              2314100300050 
                   SAMMY fitting error 0.6 %.                     2314100300051 
                   Errors in the abundances of 240Pu 4.4 %.       2314100300052 
                   Errors in the evaluated value of JENDL-4.0 of  2314100300053 
           the first resonance of 240Pu 2.2 %.                    2314100300054 
                   Systematic errors in influences of the         2314100300055 
           scattered neutrons 0.3 0.3                             2314100300056 
           Error in the abundances of 240Pu and error in the      2314100300057 
           isotopic ratio of 244Cm to 246Cm" are not independent; 2314100300058 
           both errors include error in the isotopic ratio of     2314100300059 
           244Cm (comment of author Atsushi Kimura ).             2314100300060
